Visit & apply.

23/11/2019, 5:15 pm - Huzaifah Zia: #pragma once
#include <iostream>
#include <string>
using namespace std;
struct fes {
	int x[3] = {0};//total spending on festival
	int s = 0;//index of least spending out of the top three
	string n;//name  of festival
};
class ht {
private:
	fes* ff;
	int size;
public:
	ht() {
		size = 0;
		ff = NULL;
	}
	void sixe(int s) {
		size = s;
		ff = new fes[size];
	}
	void in() {
		string a;//a is name 
		int q, ci, d;//c is index data is stored at, d is also index data is to be stored at,q is spending
		bool w = false;
		cin >> a;
		cin >> q;
		ci = search(a);
		if (ci == -1) {
			ci = hash(a);
			d = ci;
			do {
				w = false;
				if (ff[ci].x[0] == 0) {
					ff[ci].n = a;
					ff[ci].x[0] = q;
					ff[ci].s = 0;
					w = true;
				}
				else {
					++ci;
				}
			} while (!w);
		}
		else {
			insert(ci, q);
		}
	}
	void insert(int a, int d) {//a is index,d is data to be inseted
		for (int i = 0; i < 3; ++i) {
			if (ff[a].x[i] == 0) {
				ff[a].x[i] = d;
				if (d < ff[a].x[ff[a].s]) {
					ff[a].s = i;
				}
				return;
			}
		}
		if (d > ff[a].x[ff[a].s]) {
			ff[a].x[ff[a].s] = d;
			for (int i = 0; i < 3; ++i) {
				if (d < ff[a].x[ff[a].s]) {
					ff[a].s = i;
				}
				return;
			}
		}
	}
	int search(string b) {
		for (int i = 0; i < size; ++i) {
			if (b == ff[i].n) {
				return i;
			}
		}
		return -1;
	}
	int hash(string b) {
		int a = int(b[0]);
		return (a % size);
	}
	int suml(int a) {
		int sum = 0;
		for (int i = 0; i < 3; ++i) {
			sum += ff[a].x[i];
		}
		return sum;
	}
	int largest() {
		int l = 0;
		for (int i = 1; i < size; ++i) {
			if (suml(i) == suml(l)) {
				if (ff[i].n < ff[l].n) {
					l = i;
				}
			}
			if (suml(i) > suml(l)) {
				l = i;
			}
		}
		return l;
	}
	void print() {
		int a = largest();
		cout << ff[a].n << " " << suml(a) << endl;
	}
	~ht() {
		delete[]ff;
	}
};

cout<<"Exit status of child was "<< e_status;
cout<< " and the ID is " << pid << endl;
}
}

16/04/2020, 9:53 pm - Huzaifah Zia: #include<stdio.h>
#include<iostream>
#include<unistd.h>
#include<pthread.h>
#include<sys/types.h>
#include<stdlib.h>
#include<time.h>
using namespace std;

class coffee{
private:
   pthread_mutex_t m1;
   pthread_cond_t c1,c2,c3,c4;
   int a,b;
public:
   coffee(){
     a = 0; b = 0;
     pthread_mutex_t  m1= PTHREAD_MUTEX_INITIALIZER;
     pthread_cond_t  c1= PTHREAD_COND_INITIALIZER;
     pthread_cond_t  c2= PTHREAD_COND_INITIALIZER;
     pthread_cond_t  c3= PTHREAD_COND_INITIALIZER;
     pthread_cond_t  c4= PTHREAD_COND_INITIALIZER;
   }
   void s(){//select at random
     pthread_mutex_lock(&m1);
     a = rand() % 3+1;
     do{
     b = rand() % 3+1;
     }while(b == a);
     //1 is coffee, 2 is sugar, 3 is milk
     if(((a==1) && (b==2)) || ((a==2) && (b==1))){
       cout<<"\nSending Signal to Person with milk";
       pthread_cond_signal(&c3);
       pthread_mutex_unlock(&m1);
       pthread_mutex_lock(&m1);
       pthread_cond_wait(&c4,&m1);
       pthread_mutex_unlock(&m1);
     }
     else if (((a==1) && (b==3)) || ((a==3) && (b==1))){
       cout<<"\nSending Signal to Person with sugar";
       pthread_cond_signal(&c2);
       pthread_mutex_unlock(&m1);
       pthread_mutex_lock(&m1);
       pthread_cond_wait(&c4,&m1);
       pthread_mutex_unlock(&m1);       
     }
     else if (((a==2) && (b==3)) || ((a==3) && (b==2))){
       cout<<"\nSending Signal to Person with coffee";
       pthread_cond_signal(&c1);
       pthread_mutex_unlock(&m1);
       pthread_mutex_lock(&m1);
       pthread_cond_wait(&c4,&m1);
       pthread_mutex_unlock(&m1);       
     }
     else{
       pthread_mutex_unlock(&m1);
     }
   }
   void mak_s(){//Person with sugar makes coffee
     pthread_cond_wait(&c2,&m1);
     cout << "\nPerson with sugar Makes coffee.";
     pthread_cond_signal(&c4);
   }
   void mak_c(){//person with coffee makes coffee
     pthread_cond_wait(&c1,&m1);
     cout << "\nPerson with coffee Makes coffee.";
     pthread_cond_signal(&c4);
   }
   void mak_m(){//person with milk makes coffee
     pthread_cond_wait(&c3,&m1);
     cout << "\nPerson with milk Makes coffee.";
     pthread_cond_signal(&c4);
   }
}cofe;

void* agent(void* var){
  while(1)
  cofe.s();
  sleep(1);
}

void* sugar(void* var){
  while(1)
  cofe.mak_s();
  sleep(1);
}

void* cof(void* var){
  while(1)
  cofe.mak_c();
  sleep(1);
}

void* milk(void* var){
  while(1)
  cofe.mak_m();
  sleep(1);
}

int main(void){
    pthread_t p1, p2, p3, a;
    srand(time(NULL));
    pthread_create(&a,NULL,agent,NULL);
    pthread_create(&p1,NULL,sugar,NULL);
    pthread_create(&p2,NULL,cof,NULL);
    pthread_create(&p3,NULL,milk,NULL);
    pthread_exit(NULL);
    return 0;
}

15/06/2021, 10:45 am - Huzaifah Zia: #include <mpi.h>
#include <stdio.h>
#include <math.h>

void BCast(int d, int id, int X);

int main(int argc, char** argv) {
    // Initialize the MPI environment
    MPI_Init(&argc,&argv);
    
 MPI_Status status;	
    // Get the number of processes -> how many processes are to be created
    int p;
	int i;
	//MPI_COMM_WORLD is an communicator object that contains all the processes
    MPI_Comm_size(MPI_COMM_WORLD, &p);

    // Get the rank of the process -> it is the process id
    int my_rank;
	
    MPI_Comm_rank(MPI_COMM_WORLD, &my_rank);
    //Broadcasting message assuming it as a hypercube
    double d = log(p)/log(2);
    printf("%f\n",d);
    BCast(d,my_rank, 10);
    // Finalize the MPI environment.
    MPI_Finalize();
}

void BCast(int d, int id, int X){
	MPI_Status status;
	int dest = 0, tag = 1, recv, source=0;
	int mask = (pow(2,d)-1);
	for (int i = d-1; i>=0; --i){
		int w = pow(2,i);
		mask = mask^w;
		if ((id&mask) == 0) {
			if ((id&w) == 0) {
				dest = id^w;
				printf("Process:%d is sending \'%d\' to process:%d \n",id, X,dest);
				MPI_Send(&X, 1, MPI_INT, dest, tag, MPI_COMM_WORLD);
			}
			else{
				MPI_Recv(&recv, 1, MPI_INT, source, tag, MPI_COMM_WORLD, &status);
				printf("Process:%d has received \'%d\' from process:%d\n",id, recv, source);
			}
		}
	}
}

19/07/2021, 3:12 pm - Abdullah (B): import numpy as np
import matplotlib.pyplot as plt
import pandas as pd
from sklearn.preprocessing import LabelEncoder
from sklearn.model_selection import train_test_split
from sklearn.preprocessing import StandardScaler
from keras.wrappers.scikit_learn import KerasClassifier
from sklearn.model_selection import GridSearchCV
from keras.models import Sequential
from keras.layers import Dense
from keras.models import Sequential
from keras.layers import Dense
from keras.models import load_model
from sklearn.metrics import confusion_matrix

dataset = pd.read_csv('Spiraldata.csv')

def dataAnalysis(df):
    # DataSet Head
    print("Dataset Head")
    print(df.head(3))
    print("=" * 30)

    # Features
    print("Dataset Features")
    print(df.columns.values)
    print("=" * 30)

    # Samples and Missing Values
    print("Dataset Features Details")
    print(df.info())
    print("=" * 30)

    # Numerical Features
    print("Dataset Numerical Features")
    print(df.describe())
    print("=" * 30)

    # Categorical Features
    print("Dataset Categorical Features")
    print(df.describe(include=['O']))
    print("=" * 30)

dataAnalysis(dataset)

X = dataset.iloc[:,2:32] 
y = dataset.iloc[:,1] 

print("Before encoding: ")
print(y[100:110])

labelencoder_Y = LabelEncoder()
y = labelencoder_Y.fit_transform(y)

print("\nAfter encoding: ")
print(y[100:110])

# Splitting Dataset
X_train, X_test, y_train, y_test = train_test_split(X, y, test_size = 0.2, random_state = 0)

# Features Scaling
sc = StandardScaler()
X_train = sc.fit_transform(X_train)
X_test = sc.transform(X_test)

# Tuning Hyper parameters
def build_classifier(optimizer):
    classifier = Sequential()
    classifier.add(Dense(units = 16, kernel_initializer = 'uniform', activation = 'relu', input_dim = 30))
    classifier.add(Dense(units = 8, kernel_initializer = 'uniform', activation = 'relu'))
    classifier.add(Dense(units = 6, kernel_initializer = 'uniform', activation = 'relu'))
    classifier.add(Dense(units = 1, kernel_initializer = 'uniform', activation = 'sigmoid'))
    classifier.compile(optimizer = optimizer, loss = 'binary_crossentropy', metrics = ['accuracy'])
    return classifier

classifier = KerasClassifier(build_fn = build_classifier)
parameters = {'batch_size': [1, 5],
              'epochs': [100, 120],
              'optimizer': ['adam', 'rmsprop']}
grid_search = GridSearchCV(estimator = classifier,
                           param_grid = parameters,
                           scoring = 'accuracy',
                           cv = 10)
grid_search = grid_search.fit(X_train, y_train)

best_parameters = grid_search.best_params_
best_accuracy = grid_search.best_score_
print("best_parameters: ")
print(best_parameters)
print("\nbest_accuracy: ")
print(best_accuracy)

# Building Neural Network
classifier = Sequential()
classifier.add(Dense(units = 16, kernel_initializer = 'uniform', activation = 'relu', input_dim = 30))
classifier.add(Dense(units = 8, kernel_initializer = 'uniform', activation = 'relu'))
classifier.add(Dense(units = 6, kernel_initializer = 'uniform', activation = 'relu'))
classifier.add(Dense(units = 1, kernel_initializer = 'uniform', activation = 'sigmoid'))

# Compiling ANN
classifier.compile(optimizer = 'rmsprop', loss = 'binary_crossentropy', metrics = ['accuracy'])

# Fitting Data
classifier.fit(X_train, y_train, batch_size = 1, epochs = 100)

# Saving and Loading the Model
classifier.save('breast_cancer_model.h5') 
classifier = load_model('breast_cancer_model.h5') 

# Making Predictions
# Assign the results true or false based on their probabilities
y_pred = classifier.predict(X_test)
y_pred = [ 1 if y>=0.5 else 0 for y in y_pred ]

# Printing the confusion matrix
cm = confusion_matrix(y_test, y_pred)
print(cm)

accuracy = (cm[0][0]+cm[1][1])/(cm[0][0]+cm[0][1]+cm[1][0]+cm[1][1])
print("Accuracy: "+ str(accuracy*100)+"%")
